 aviation export harshavardhan kehete hai, 'ye leen sijan hota he kyonki skool ke exam hote hai or log zyada safar nahin karte
 In such a situation, the load factor increases with these offers
 'aane vaale dinon main desh ke bazaar main kuch nai airlines bhi pankh pasaarne ke sanket de chuki hai
 It is believed that in such a situation, these attractive offers are the way to save the market share of the airlines currently working and to keep themselves connected with the passengers
 harshavardhan kehete hai, 'air asia bazaar main utarane hi vaali he aise main ye ofer apana market share bachaae rakhane kii kavayad he taaki aane vaali airline ko mushkil ho or uskaa 'jestation period' bhi bade
 With the offer of cheap tickets, new passengers also join the airlines, so this also gives hope to the airlines to increase passenger base
 khap mahapanchayat ne samaan gotra main vivaah par roak lagane ke makasad se sanvaidhanik sanshodhan karne ke liye aaj apana andolan tej karne kaa faisla kiya or kaha ki is tarah ke vivaah parampara or saamaajik mandandon ke khilaaf hote hai
 Khap representatives of various castes took part in the Sarvakhap Mahapanchayat, an ethnic race held here
 isamen pran kiya gaya ki hindu vivaah adhinium 1955 main sanshodhan hone tak andolan jari rakhaa jaayegaa
 a resolution criticizing the Union ministers who were opposed to this demand was also passed in the Mahapanchayat
 loksabhaa chunaavon ke paanch charan sampann ho chuke hai

 is bich gujarat ke congress netaa hardik patel ne mangalvaar ko pradhanmantri narendra modi par nishaanaa saadhaa he
 Hardik Patel has said that after the fifth phase of the ongoing Lok Sabha elections in the country, the people of this country have decided that the Congress government should be formed in 2019
 isliye pradhanmantri narendra modi ke chehre se hansi gaayab ho gai he
 Hardik Patel also claimed that not only will Congress President Rahul Gandhi become the Prime Minister of the country, but in this Lok Sabha election, Congress will win more seats than BJP in Gujarat
 hardik ne bhopal main media se baat karte hue kaha, ‘is baar janata mudde ke saath he, ahimsa ke saath he
 i believe that the people of the country have relied on Rahul and the Congress Party
 ’ unhone aage kaha, ‘is desh kii janata ne tay kar liya he ki 2019 main congress party kii sarkaar banani he

 ye baat alag he ki ham sab kabhi-kabhi apni is rekha ko langhakar aage nikalne kii koshish karte hai, lekin der saver is baat kaa ehsaas ho hi jaataa ki patrakarita kaa mul siddhant hi aaj bhi praasangik he ki report karen naa ki jajment den
 Therefore, i too am telling what i have seen, heard and felt
 22 april buudhvaar ko main subah hi jantar mantar par aam aadmi party kii kisaan raily cover karne pahunch gaya
 The crowd had started gathering since morning and then when it was about noon, my eyes fell on a man climbing a neem tree
 mujhe wo thodaa alag isliye laga kyonki aamtaur par jantar mantar par jo log ped par chadhakar raily yaa dharne pradarshan kaa anand lete hai wo utani oonchai par nahin jate jitani par wo chalaa gaya tha
 It was now noon, the leaders of the AAP were giving a turn-by-turn speech that suddenly when i was in the media enclosure, a man tried to bring my attention to the tree but i could not understand and he said 'your country Also awesome, here is one to one '(he hinted but i did not understand anything and did not see anything)
 lekin thodi der baar meri nazar usee shaks par padi jisko maine ped ke upar chadhate dekha tha
 Now i also understand what a person was telling me a few moments ago, about a man who has climbed on the same tree ('apna Desh is awesome, here is one to one)
 ' i focused on the tree and saw that the farmer put a noose around his neck and it seemed that he was probably shouting some slogans
 kuch der tak maine us par nazar banaae rakhi or mujhe laga ki shaayad ye apni taraf dhyaan kheenchna chahta he yaa kuch kahana chahta he yaa ho saktaa he isaki maansik sthiti thik naa ho(kyonki aksar reliyon yaa pradarshnon main aise maamle dekhe jate hai jo baad main koi gambhir masalaa nahin dikhte)
 Now i set my eyes just below the same tree, then there the guest teacher appeared busy in his performance but then i focused more properly and saw that most of the people in the same area, just below the tree, were the guest teacher, that banner or poster Performing with hand in hand
 duusare kuch log tali bajaakar yaa manch kii ore haath hilaakar us faansee lagaae shaks kii ore dhyaan dilaane kii koshish kar rahe the
 (till now all the focus was on the guest teachers in the rally) ab manch par kumaar vishwaas bolne aae or unhone sabase pehle guest teacheron ko sambodhit kiya or unako kaha ki is tarah se pradarshan karne se kuch nahin hoga, shiksha mantri aapse pehle bhi mili hai or aage bhi milenge or kisaan raily main jameen adhigrahan jaise gambhir mudde ke bich is tarah ke pradarshan kaa kuch matlab nikaala jayega
 Shortly thereafter, Kumar Vishwas appealed to the man who was climbing the tree and hugging the noose
 kumaar ne us aadmi se apil kii ki kripaya neeche aa jaaen or jo baat kahana chaahate hai kahie or police se apil kii ki kripaya isko neeche utaariye
 When i put my eyes back on the man, i saw that he was holding the noose with his two hands with a noose around his neck with which he tied the noose and there is also a twig near his left leg which is supporting him
 jab police harakat main nahin ai to kumaar vishwaas ne police par kisi ke ishaare par yojanabaddh tareeke se kaam karne kaa aarope lagaaya
 Where i was standing and as far as i could see, i saw the policemen becoming mute spectators
 kahin aisa nahin dikhaa ki police koi koshish kar rahi ho ped par chadhakar us aadmi ko bachaane kii
 After this, some people climbed the tree and started trying to take down the man, and by their efforts, they felt that it was not an expert to deal with such a situation
 us aadmi ko jaise taise ped se utaara gaya, aspataal ke liye ravaanaa kiya gaya
 After that, i saw people coming down from the tree, in which the Banda coming down in a white cloth started crying on the tree, then the rest of the people hugged him and pacified him
 (haalanki wo royaa kyon or wo he koun ye mujhe baad main pataa chalaa
 He was a volunteer of AAP who tried to save the man and i interviewed him too
 ) The meeting was halted for a while
 is puri ghatana ke dauraan or jab usko aspataal bhej diya gaya to sabha phir shuru hui
 i stayed at my place on the stage made for the media and made sure to keep my cameraperson there as there were thousands of people between me and that neem tree and what i would do there, increase the crowd and hinder any possible efforts The Because i do not even know how to climb a tree and also talk that when someone is in an attempt to commit suicide, they have to be persuaded and persuaded or else the matter may be bad, so only an expert can do this work
 is bich vahaan maujuud logon main bas yahi charchaa chalati rahi ki wo aadmi batch gaya yaa mar gaya
 The news that came to me was that the condition is very bad
 mere anubhav ne kaha ki wo zindaa he yaa nahin ye doctor bataaenge, ham kaise bataaen(kyonki jab tak main raily main maujuud rahaa kabhi khabar ai ki wo batch gaya to kabhi khabar ai ki wo nahin rahaa)
 When the meeting proceeded, my focus was now on two things
 ek to guest teacher jo badi sankhya main subah se hi pradarshan karne aae the or kar rahe the or ab doosraa wo aadmi jo aatmahatya kaa prayaas kar rahaa tha wo ab jivit he yaa nahin
 When Arvind Kejriwal came to speak in the last, he first spoke about the man and then gave a speech about ten to fifteen minutes on the issue of farmers
 lekin is dauraan jo subah se ashankit tha, guest teacheron ne apana pradarshan tej kiya or kaale jhande dikhaane lage or in sabake bich raily samaapt hui
 CM Kejriwal and deputy CM Sisodia left for the hospital
 tippaniyan Further story and analysis in the next section

 disclemur (asveekaran) : is aalekh main vyakt kiye gaye vichaar lekhak ke nijee vichaar hai
 NDTV is not responsible for the accuracy, completeness, practicality or truthfulness of any information provided in this article
 is aalekh main sabhi suchanaaen jyon kii tyon prastut kii gai hai
 None of the information or facts or views expressed in this article are of NDTV, and NDTV is not responsible for them in any way
 ab dopaher kaa samay tha, manch par aap ke netaa baari-baari se bhaashan de rahe the ki achaanak jab main media encloger main tha to ek aadmi ne meraa dhyaan ped par dilaane kii koshish kii lekin mujhe samaj nahin aayaa or usne kaha 'apana desh bhi kamaal he, yahaan ek se ek hai' (usne ishaara to kiya lekin mujhe naa kuch samaj aayaa or naa kuch dikhaai diya)
 But for a while my eyes fell on the person i saw climbing on the tree
 ab meri samaj main wo baat bhi ai ki kuch kshan pehle ek shaks mujhe kya kah rahaa tha, isi ped ke upar chadhe shaks ke bare main('apana desh bhi kamaal he, yahaan ek se ek hai)
 ' maine ped par nazar focus kii or dekha ki us kisaan ne gale main ek fanda daal rakhaa he or lag rahaa tha ki wo shaayad kuch naare laga rahaa tha
 i kept an eye on it for a while and i felt that it might want to draw attention to itself or say something or it might not have a good mental state (because in rallies or demonstrations, such cases are often seen
 i do not see any serious issues)
 ab maine apni nazaren usee ped ke thik neeche lagaai to vahaan par guest teacher apane pradarshan main vyast dikhe lekin phir maine or thik se focus kiya to dekha ki usee ilaake main yani ped ke thik neeche zyaadaatar log jo guest teacher the, wo binar yaa poster haath main lekar pradarshan kar rahe the
 Some others were trying to draw attention to the person hanging by clapping or shaking hands towards the stage
 (abhi tak raily main guest teacheron par hi sabakaa dhyaan kendrit tha) Now Kumar Vishwas came to speak on the stage and he first addressed the guest teachers and told them that such a demonstration would do nothing, the Education Minister has met you before and will meet further and serious issues like land acquisition in Kisan rally Such a demonstration would be interpreted as something between
 iske thik baad kumaar vishwaas ne us aadmi se apil kii jo ped par chadhakar faansee kaa fanda gale main daale hue tha
 Kumar appealed to the man to come down and say whatever he wanted to say and appealed to the police to take it down
 maine apni nazaren waapas us aadmi par lagaai to dekha ki usne gale main fanda daalkar apane donon haathon se usee daali ko pakadaa hua he jisase usne fanda baandha tha or uske baayen pair ke paas bhi ek tahani he jisase usko saport mil rahaa he
 When the police did not act, Kumar Vishwas accused the police of acting in a planned manner at someone's behest
 jahaan par main khadaa tha or jahaan tak main dekh paaya, mujhe pulisavaale mookadarshak bane dikhaai diye
 Nowhere does it appear that the police is trying to save the man by climbing a tree
 iske baad kuch log ped par chadhe or us aadmi ko utaarne kii koshish karne lage or unki koshish se laga ki ye koi export nahin, is tarah ke halaat se nipatane ke
 The man was rushed to the hospital as soon as he was lowered from the tree
 uske baad maine logon ko ped se neeche utarate dekha jisamen ek safed kapadon main neeche aata banda ped par hi rone laga to baaki logon ne usko gale lagaakar shant kiya
 (though i cried later and i came to know who he is
 wo 'aap' kaa walantier tha jisane us aadmi ko bachaane kii koshish kii or maine uskaa intervyuu bhi kiya
 ) kuch der ke liye sabha rukii hui thi
 The meeting resumed during this entire incident and when he was sent to the hospital
 main apni jagah par vahiin media ke liye banaae gaye stage par rahaa or apane cameraperson ko bhi vahiin rakhana sunishchit kiya kyonki mere or us neem ke ped ke bich hazaron log the or vahaan jaakar main karata kya, bheed badhaata or kisi sambhavit koshish main baadha banataa? kyonki mujhe to ped par chadhana bhi nahin aata or saath main baat ye bhi ki jab koi aatmahatya ke prayaas main hota he to usko rijhaanaa or manaanaa padataa he varna maamla kharaab bhi ho saktaa he, isliye ye kaam koi export hi kar saktaa he
 In the meantime, there was only discussion among the people present whether the man survived or died
 mere paas jo khabar ai wo ye thi ki haalat behad kharaab he
 My experience said that the doctor will tell whether he is alive or not, how can we tell (because as long as i was present in the rally, there was news that he survived, sometimes it was reported that he was not)
 jab sabha aage badi to ab meraa dhyaan do baton par tha
 One was the guest teacher who had come and performed in large numbers since morning and now the other man who was trying to commit suicide is now alive or not
 jab aakhri main arvind kejariwal bolne aae to pehle unhone us aadmi ke bare main bolaa or phir kisaanon ke mudde par kareeb das pandrah minute bhaashan diya
 But during this period, which had been apprehensive since morning, the guest teachers stepped up their display and started showing black flags and the rally ended among them all
 siem kejariwal or dipti siem sisodiya aspataal ke liye ravaanaa hue
 The comments aage kii kahani or vishleshan agle hisse main

 The meeting resumed during this entire incident and when he was sent to the hospital
 main apni jagah par vahiin media ke liye banaae gaye stage par rahaa or apane cameraperson ko bhi vahiin rakhana sunishchit kiya kyonki mere or us neem ke ped ke bich hazaron log the or vahaan jaakar main karata kya, bheed badhaata or kisi sambhavit koshish main baadha banataa? kyonki mujhe to ped par chadhana bhi nahin aata or saath main baat ye bhi ki jab koi aatmahatya ke prayaas main hota he to usko rijhaanaa or manaanaa padataa he varna maamla kharaab bhi ho saktaa he, isliye ye kaam koi export hi kar saktaa he
 In the meantime, there was only discussion among the people present whether the man survived or died
 mere paas jo khabar ai wo ye thi ki haalat behad kharaab he
 My experience said that the doctor will tell whether he is alive or not, how can we tell (because as long as i was present in the rally, there was news that he survived, sometimes it was reported that he was not)
 jab sabha aage badi to ab meraa dhyaan do baton par tha
 One was the guest teacher who had come and performed in large numbers since morning and now the other man who was trying to commit suicide is now alive or not
 jab aakhri main arvind kejariwal bolne aae to pehle unhone us aadmi ke bare main bolaa or phir kisaanon ke mudde par kareeb das pandrah minute bhaashan diya
 But during this period, which had been apprehensive since morning, the guest teachers stepped up their display and started showing black flags and the rally ended among them all
 siem kejariwal or dipti siem sisodiya aspataal ke liye ravaanaa hue
 The comments aage kii kahani or vishleshan agle hisse main

 is aalekh main di gai kisi bhi soochna kii sateekta, sampoornataa, vyaavhaarikta athwa sachai ke prati enditivi uttaradaayi nahin he
 All the information in this article is presented as it is
 is aalekh main di gai koi bhi soochna athwa tathy athwa vyakt kiye gaye vichaar enditivi ke nahin hai, tathaa enditivi unke liye kisi bhi prakaar se uttaradaayi nahin he
 i focused on the tree and saw that the farmer put a noose around his neck and it seemed that he was probably shouting some slogans
 kuch der tak maine us par nazar banaae rakhi or mujhe laga ki shaayad ye apni taraf dhyaan kheenchna chahta he yaa kuch kahana chahta he yaa ho saktaa he isaki maansik sthiti thik naa ho(kyonki aksar reliyon yaa pradarshnon main aise maamle dekhe jate hai jo baad main koi gambhir masalaa nahin dikhte)
 Now i set my eyes just below the same tree, then there the guest teacher appeared busy in his performance but then i focused more properly and saw that most of the people in the same area, just below the tree, were the guest teacher, that banner or poster Performing with hand in hand
 duusare kuch log tali bajaakar yaa manch kii ore haath hilaakar us faansee lagaae shaks kii ore dhyaan dilaane kii koshish kar rahe the
 (till now all the focus was on the guest teachers in the rally) ab manch par kumaar vishwaas bolne aae or unhone sabase pehle guest teacheron ko sambodhit kiya or unako kaha ki is tarah se pradarshan karne se kuch nahin hoga, shiksha mantri aapse pehle bhi mili hai or aage bhi milenge or kisaan raily main jameen adhigrahan jaise gambhir mudde ke bich is tarah ke pradarshan kaa kuch matlab nikaala jayega
 Shortly thereafter, Kumar Vishwas appealed to the man who was climbing the tree and hugging the noose
 kumaar ne us aadmi se apil kii ki kripaya neeche aa jaaen or jo baat kahana chaahate hai kahie or police se apil kii ki kripaya isko neeche utaariye
 When i put my eyes back on the man, i saw that he was holding the noose with his two hands with a noose around his neck with which he tied the noose and there is also a twig near his left leg which is supporting him
 jab police harakat main nahin ai to kumaar vishwaas ne police par kisi ke ishaare par yojanabaddh tareeke se kaam karne kaa aarope lagaaya
 Where i was standing and as far as i could see, i saw the policemen becoming mute spectators
 kahin aisa nahin dikhaa ki police koi koshish kar rahi ho ped par chadhakar us aadmi ko bachaane kii
 After this, some people climbed the tree and started trying to take down the man, and by their efforts, they felt that it was not an expert to deal with such a situation
 us aadmi ko jaise taise ped se utaara gaya, aspataal ke liye ravaanaa kiya gaya
 After that, i saw people coming down from the tree, in which the Banda coming down in a white cloth started crying on the tree, then the rest of the people hugged him and pacified him
 (haalanki wo royaa kyon or wo he koun ye mujhe baad main pataa chalaa
 He was a volunteer of AAP who tried to save the man and i interviewed him too
 ) The meeting was halted for a while
 is puri ghatana ke dauraan or jab usko aspataal bhej diya gaya to sabha phir shuru hui
 i stayed at my place on the stage made for the media and made sure to keep my cameraperson there as there were thousands of people between me and that neem tree and what i would do there, increase the crowd and hinder any possible efforts The Because i do not even know how to climb a tree and also talk that when someone is in an attempt to commit suicide, they have to be persuaded and persuaded or else the matter may be bad, so only an expert can do this work
 is bich vahaan maujuud logon main bas yahi charchaa chalati rahi ki wo aadmi batch gaya yaa mar gaya
 The news that came to me was that the condition is very bad
 mere anubhav ne kaha ki wo zindaa he yaa nahin ye doctor bataaenge, ham kaise bataaen(kyonki jab tak main raily main maujuud rahaa kabhi khabar ai ki wo batch gaya to kabhi khabar ai ki wo nahin rahaa)
 When the meeting proceeded, my focus was now on two things
 ek to guest teacher jo badi sankhya main subah se hi pradarshan karne aae the or kar rahe the or ab doosraa wo aadmi jo aatmahatya kaa prayaas kar rahaa tha wo ab jivit he yaa nahin
 When Arvind Kejriwal came to speak in the last, he first spoke about the man and then gave a speech about ten to fifteen minutes on the issue of farmers
 lekin is dauraan jo subah se ashankit tha, guest teacheron ne apana pradarshan tej kiya or kaale jhande dikhaane lage or in sabake bich raily samaapt hui
 CM Kejriwal and deputy CM Sisodia left for the hospital

 In Uttar Pradesh and Bihar politics, once again the election movement is about to start
 in donon rajyon kii vidhaan parishad kii 24 siten agle maheene may main khaali hone ja rahi hai or ise 6 may se pehle bharaa janaa he
 In a press release issued by the Election Commission, it was told that in the Legislative Council elections held every 2 years, 13 seats from UP and 11 seats from Bihar are going to be vacant this year
 uttar pradeshmen 13 sadasyon kaa kaarykaal 5 may ko khatm hone ja rahaa he jabaki bihar main 6 may ko khatm hoga
 Some very big names are also included in these seats
 bihar main mukhyamantri niteesha kumaar, upmukhyamantri susheel kumaar modi orpurv mukhyamantri rabari devike alaava uttar pradesh ke purv mukhyamantri akhilesh yadav bhi is saal ritair hone vaali list main shaamil bada naam hai
 There will be no obstacle in the way of Chief Minister Nitish and Deputy Chief Minister Sushil Modi in Bihar to get re-elected, the same situation is also with Akhilesh
 in logon ke phir se chune jane kii sambhaavna he
 Apart from Akhilesh, Ambika Chaudhary, Umar Ali Khan, Mohsin Raza, Naresh Chandra Uttam, Madhu Gupta, Dr
 Mahendra Kumar Singh, Chaudhary Mushtaq, Rajendra Chaudhary, Ram Sakal Gurjar, Dr
 Vijay Yadav, Sunil Kumar among the 13 members of the UP Legislative Council
 And the doctor is Vijay Pratap
 duusari ore, bihar ke mukhyamantri niteesha kumaar kaa bhi kaarykaal isi samay khatm ho rahaa he
 Apart from Nitish from Bihar, Upendra Prasad, Chandreshwar Prasad, Mangal Pandey, Rabri Devi, Raj Kishore Singh Kushwaha, Lal Babu Prasad, Satyendra Narayan Singh, Sanjay Singh and Sushil Kumar Modi are included, while MLC Narendra Singh was disqualified in 2016 itself
 Were, whose time will also be completed on 6 May
 unhone kaha ki aisa lagata he ki aresas ne modi ko yah sikhaaya he ki unhen bhaashan dene par adhik jor dena chahie
 Apart from this, the RSS has taught them to stand, hold sticks, wear shorts and lie
 mere khyaal se pradhanmantri ko ab is baat kaa ehsaas ho gaya he ki nafrat, lathi, bhaashanon or jhuthe vaadon se desh nahin chalaaya ja saktaa
 (from input language) in sab baton ke aadhaar par sau se zyaada hastiyon ne raashtrapati ko dayaa yachika saunpi he

 iske alaava kai netaa, abhinaytaon or samajaseviyon ke bhi isamen dastakhat shaamil hai

 sinha ke alaava, is yachika par hastakshar karne waalon main ram jethmalani manishankar ayyar (congress), majid memon (rakanpa), seetaram yechuri (makapa), di raja (bhakpa), keties tulsi or echke dua (manonith) or tii shiva (diemke) jaise saansadon, makapa ke purv mahasachiv prakaash karaat, bhakpa (emel) libration ke mahasachiv dipankar bhattacharya, brunda karaat (makapa), nasiruddin shah, mahesh bhatta, emke raina or tushaar gandhi jaise log shaamil hai

 # PK There is silence in Meerasarai village of Azamgarh district of Uttar Pradesh
 yah sannata abu salem ke bhagya ko lekar he
 Salem, a special TADA court, is hearing the 1993 Mumbai bomb blast accused
 vishesh tada adaalat ne us par aarope tay kar die hai, lekin sajaa sunaane ke liye somvaar kaa din tay kiya gaya he
 In such a situation, the reporter went to Salem's village and talked to the people there
 parivaaravaalon ne nahin ki bauebu salem kaa ghar bilkul viraan sa tha
 The reporter knocked on the door of the house
 ghar ke andar se ek ladki ai, jo ki bahut bhaybheet dikh rahi thi
 He said that there is no one inside the house
 kaha ki ghar kaa koi shaks press se baat karnaa nahin chahta
 There is a mosque near his house, where a little uproar was seen
 log us vakt namaaj ke liye ikkatha ho rahen thea
 After the end of Namaz, people on the team till today start looking suspiciously
 jab ve vahaan pahunche to logon ne ek swar main bolaa kii abu salem nirdosh he
 People said that he was being implicated under the conspiracy
 kisi ko bhi khabar nahin thi ki salem portugal kaise pahunch gaya
 After which he was brought to India
 ilaake main salem ke khilaadek bhi cese nahidbu salem ke ek padosi mohammad asif kaa kahana tha ki 'abu salem nirdosh he
 There is a conspiracy against him
 ham bas is baat ki ummid kar rahe hai ki kisi din bas sach saamne aa jaae
 'another neighbor Abu Ubaid said that' There is not a single case against Abu Salem in this entire area
 aap jaakar police stesan se puch lijiye
 Hindus and Muslims live side by side in this area and there has not been a single riot yet
 main maanata hum ki uske khilaaf sajeesh hui he
 'ready to help everyone' The people of Abu Salem's family showed no interest in talking to the press
 parivaaravaalon main is puure maamle par bas ek udasin shanti dikhi
 Salem's neighbors should be seen with him and his family on this whole issue
 mumbai jaakar abu salem kya karata tha, is bare main jyadatar logon ko kuch bhi pataa nahin he
 People know Salem as a man who can do different kinds of work and is ready to help everyone
 abu salem ke khilaaf hue jaanch or sabooton par kai yuvyon ne sawaal uthaaya
 They pointed out that it is very easy for the police to accuse someone and collect evidence against them
 mohammad ubar ne is baat ke bhi sanket die he ki agar parivaar ke log ucch nyaayalayon main jane ke liye raji hote hai to pados ke log unke saath khadey rahenge
 a central government committee has recommended a ban on private sector crypto currencies such as bitcoin
 yah nijee kshetra ke krypto karency sanchalit karne waalon or starop ke liye bada jhatka sabit ho saktaa he
 According to the proposal, those who buy and sell it can be punished for 10 years
 ek antar mantralayan samiti (IMC) ne sabhi nijee krypto karency ko gaiyr kanoonee ghoshit karne or virtual karency se judi gatividhiyon ko aapraadhik karrwai ghoshit karne kii maang kii he
 If the government accepts the recommendation of this committee, then all such digital currency except a government crypto currency can be banned
 is kamity ke chairman aarthik maamalon ke sachiv the
 Apart from him, the committee included the secretaries of the Ministry of Electronics and Information Technology, the chairman of SEBI and the deputy governor of the Reserve Bank
 samiti ne is baat kii bhi sifarish kii he ki ek sarkari digital karency (odisi) kii shuruyaat kii jaae or use rigerv bank ke regulation main chalaakar kanoonee darja diya jaae
 The report of this committee was submitted to the government on Monday and a bill draft has also been submitted with it
 sarkaar sambandhit mantralayon or regulatory athurities ke sahyog se iemasi kii is report or bill ke praaroop kii samiksha or akalan karne ke baad hi is par koi antim nirnay legi
 The format of 'banning of Crypto Currency and Regulation of Official Digital Currency Bill, 2019' and copy of IMC report is listed on the website of Department of Economic Affairs, Ministry of Finance
 report ke anusaar duniya bhar main bitcoin, riplad, atherum or cardno jaise kareeb 2,116 krypto karency prachlit hai, jinka bazaar puunjikaran 119
 46 billion dollars
 samiti ne apni report main kaha he, 'jahaan tak nijee kshetra ke krypto karency kii baat he, unke saath jude jokhim or unki keemton main utaar-chadhaav ko dekhte hue samiti ne bharat main krypto karency ko bain karne kii sifarish kii he or bharat main krypto karency se judi kisi bhi gatividhi ko sanchalit karne waalon ke liye jurmaana or fine lagane kii bhi sifarish kii he
 IMC has also recommended to constitute a standing committee for further consideration of crypto currency matters
 samiti ne un sabhi digital rupee, yaa digital videshi mudra ko bain karne laayak krypto karency mana he, jinhen rigerv bank ke regulation ke tahat sanchalit nahin kiya ja rahaa
 The committee said that the purpose of currency is not served in any way by crypto currency and they do not have legal validity in any country
 sarkaar ne krypto karency se jude masalon par vichaar ke liye november, 2017 main is antar mantralayan samiti kaa gathan kiya tha
 What is digital or crypto currency? Crypto currency is a currency that is built on computer algorithms
 yah ek swatantra mudra he jiskaa koi maalik nahin hota
 This currency is not under the control of any one authority
 digital yaa krypto karency internet par chalane vaali ek virtual karency hai
 The virtual currency on the Internet was started in January 2009 as Bitcoin
 is virtual karency kaa istemaal kar duniya ke kisi kone main kisi vyakti ko pement kiya ja saktaa he or sabase khaas baat yah he ki is bhugtan ke liye kisi bank ko madhyam banane kii bhi jarurat nahin padati
 It is based on peer to peer technology
 notebandi ke dauraan bharat main bitcoin kii keemton main kaaphi oochaal aayaa tha
 Ricky Ponting may believe that Brian Lara has won more matches for his team than Sachin Tendulkar, but the statistics tell the opposite and the Indian batsman is miles ahead of the Caribbean legend in terms of winning matches for his team
 Huh
 ponting ne haal main kaha tha, sachin or lara meri najar main do behtareen ballebaaj hai
 Lara has won more matches for his team than Sachin, but if statistics are taken into account, Lara has only 24 in the West Indies
 42 fisadi test match jite hai, jabaki tendulkar ke rahete hue bharat ne 35
 Won 35 percent of Test matches
 in maichon main yadi in donon ke pradarshan ko dekhte hai to phir lara ke kul ranon ke 24

 01 pratishat he

 Is 01 percent

 52 percent) were able to win the West Indies

 28 percent

 Tendulkar in his career so far scored 5887 runs in 72 draw matches, including 20 centuries, while West Indies drew 36 matches while Lara
 inamen baayen haath ke is ballebaaj ne 3708 ran banaae or 12 shatak thoke
 The batsman scored 751 runs including three centuries in the eight matches that West Indies won against Australia during Lara
 isi tarah se england ke khilaaf unki maujuudagi main westeindies ne nau match jite or inamen lara keval ek shatak laga paae the
 During Lara, the Caribbean team won four matches from India and two from South Africa and Sri Lanka, but in none of these matches did Lara score a century

 pakistani suraksha balon ne aaj ek baar phir sangharsh viraam kaa ulanghan karte hue poonch jile main niyantran rekha ke paas kai bhartiya chaukiyon ko apana nishaanaa banaaya
 Pakistan attacked rockets with rockets, mortar bombs and light machine guns
 kal raat ke baad se poonch main pakistani suraksha balon kii ore se sangharsh viraam ke ulanghan kaa yah doosraa maamla he
 Pakistan started its operation last night at quarter past 12, which lasted for about two hours
 pakistani suraksha balon ne is dauraan poonch ke keji up sector par lagbhag 45 rocket or 40 mortar daage
 After this, firing from light machine guns started across the border
 brigadier general staff (bijies), 16 corps, brigadier es dua ne bataaya ki pakistan kii ore se aaj subah lagbhag saadhe chah baje ek baar phir jile ke krishnagati up sector main baari golibari ke saath rocket or mortar daage gaye
 He said that no one has been harmed by this action
 brigadier dua ne kaha ‘yah spasht taur par bina uksaave ke kii gai karrwai or sangharsh viraam kaa ulanghan tha
 He said that the Indian security forces deployed along the border also retaliated by handling the situation, which led to firing from both sides for about an hour
 dua ne bataaya ki donon ore se golibari main janmaal kaa koi nuksaan nahin hua he
 There is no news of any injuries
 unhone kaha ‘yah sangharsh viraam kaa ulanghan tha, jiskaa uddeshy seemaa ke is ore aatankwaadiyon kii ghuspaith kii koshish thi
 Pakistani security forces opened fire from Roja, Battal, Pimple and Daku posts to target the sub-divisions of Naveli, Nagi Tekri, Kranti, Kirpan, Chhajja, Gorda and Balnoi
 is saal yah paanchavin baar he, jab pakistani suraksha balon ne bhartiya chaukiyon par rocket or mortar se hamale kiye hai
 Indian wrestlers held their dominance for the third consecutive day at the 20th Commonwealth Games on Thursday, winning a total of four medals, including two golds
 olympics padak vijeta yogshwar dutt or mahila varg se babitha kumari ne guuruuvaar ko bharat ko swarna dilaayaa, jabaki geetika jakhad ko final mukaable main harkar rajat padak se santosh karnaa padaa
 Pawan Kumar captured the bronze as the last medal of the day in wrestling
 babitha ne scottish agsibishan conference centre (esaisisi) main mahila free style spardhaa ke 55 kilogram bharvarg ke final mukaable main canada kii britane laveredyor ko ekatarfa mukaable main maat dekar swarna padak par kabja jamaaya
 Babita, after performing brilliantly, scored five points in the first period and did not allow her opponent to score a single point
 duusare period main laveredyor do ank hasil kar sakin, lekin chaar ank hasil kar babitha is period main un par baari sabit huin
 Babita was declared the winner by 3–1 on the basis of technical points
 iske baad olympics padak vijeta yogeshwar dutt ne purush varg kii free style spardhaa ke 65 kilogram bharvarg main canada ke jevon balfor ko ekatarfa mukaable main maat dekar kushti main bharat ko paanchvaan or toornament main 12waan swarna dilaa diya
 Yogeshwar already captured 10 points in the period and captured the gold by a big margin of six points
 unke pratidwandvi balfor ek bhi ank hasil nahin kar sake
 Geetika Jakhar, who was hoping to win the third gold medal of the day for India from the women's section, however lost in the 63 kg weight category in the women's freestyle event and had to be content with the silver medal
 deepika ne canada kii apni pratidwandvi deniele lapage ke khilaaf kaaphi sangharsh kiya, lekin vah saaf-saaf lapage se damakham main kamatar najar ain
